<pics>None< /pics>< Review>
It's the candy store of personal care products. You can get high just breathing in all those amazing natural fragrances. Their products are pricey, but a little goes a long way. Two large bottles of fairly traded honey shampoo last me for a year, and I have thick long hair. Before you spend a lot of money, or are turned off by the prices and walk out of the store, ask for some samples. The staff is always friendly, knowledgeable, and helpful, and will personally fill you a few samples to try the products at home. But be aware! A small sample might get you hooked!< /Review>

I found Dr. Taban, and am very  fortunate to have done so. In terms of the revision, Dr. Taban performed a bilateral closed canthoplasty and a bilateral lower eyelid retraction. First, during the initial consultation, Dr. Taban partnered with me to decide the best course of action, providing suggestions and alternatives and likely outcomes and determining together how we were going to proceed.  He solicited and welcomed my questions and provided answers that were clear and straightforward. < review>
I could not be more grateful that I went to Doctor Taban for my eyelid surgery.

Before seeing Doctor Taban, I had seen three plastic surgeons about a mild, yet unsightly, bulge above my eyelids. All three of the previous doctors told me that I had excess fat and/or skin and that I basically needed a blepharoplasty - the most common cosmetic eyelid surgery.

My husband, who knew of Doctor Taban, insisted that I see him before we made our decision about my eyes... and thank goodness I did! Unbeknownst to me, the bulge above my eyelids was not excess fat or skin at all! It was ‚Äúprolapsed lacrimal glands‚Äù - meaning it was my tear ducts that were pushed out too far. Doctor Taban needed to simply cut open my eyelids and push my lacrimal glads (my tear ducts) back further into my eye socket (where they should be).

My surgery went perfectly. The only part that was painful, was at the beginning when shots were applied around my eyes for numbing. Other than that, the entire procedure was painless as was the recovery as well.

Now, I am completely happy with my results and am entirely grateful that I went to Doctor Taban. Seeing a very particular specialist, and someone who is the best in their field, is worth it a million times over.

-Juliet S.<//review>

<username>Hugh Byrne< /username><Time>1535338268907</Time><Rating>4<//Rating>< Review>
Excellent location, close to river and short walk to park info center and other facilities.  Spots on the east side (e.g. 20, 22, 24, 26, etc.) have creek running behind them, which is terrific.  Crowded on weekends, and spacing is close enough that things get a bit too cozy at times, particularly if you have a group of partiers next to your site, as we did, who went late into the night with beer pong and music.  Bathrooms were not attended to in our two days there, with trash getting close to full and used diapers on the floor (c'mon folks, really).  For greater privacy, stick with sites closer to the road, which are both more generously spaced and less popular.< /Review>

The food is definitely overpriced. I have been much much better sushi restaurant, which cost about half of what I paid for at this place. The waitress was also super slow in her service. It wasn't even very busy when we were there. Most of the tables next to us were empty. Yet the waitress ignored us for half an hour after we finished our entree. No one came to us until we asked another waiter to bring us the dessert menu. That's another thing! Their desserts are horrible. They were literally sugar bombs! After we finished our dessert, again the waitress ignored us for another half an hour before she brought us the check.
